[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation when processing MDTM [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmodification time[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m responses. The [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mASan[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m detected an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte read operation that overflows a global [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer by accessing memory immediately after the `Curl_seconds` global variable. [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis issue was discovered through fuzzing the curl_fuzzer_ftp target and results in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma crash with a scariness score of [0m[1;36m23[0m[39m.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **global-buffer-overflow** vulnerability, specifically an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte read [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperation that accesses memory beyond the bounds of a global variable. [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer has classified this as a READ operation with a scariness score of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m23[0m[39m.[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### What the Issue Is[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe crash occurs during FTP protocol handling when processing the MDTM response. [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe stack trace shows the following execution path:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m initiates a test case via [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`fuzz_handle_transfer`[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The execution flows through `curl_multi_perform` → `multi_runsingle` → [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`protocol_doing`[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The FTP-specific code path is triggered: `ftp_doing` → `ftp_multi_statemach` → [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ftp_statemachine`[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The crash occurs in `ftp_state_mdtm_resp` at line [0m[1;36m2107[0m[39m, column [0m[1;36m21[0m[39m of [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/curl/lib/[0m[95mftp.c[0m[39m`[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe memory access violation occurs at address `[0m[1;36m0x564a3c294240[0m[39m`, which is located [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes after the global variable `Curl_seconds` defined in [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/curl/lib/[0m[95mparsedate.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m113[0m[39m`. The `Curl_seconds` variable has a size of [0m[1;36m480[0m[39m [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes and ends exactly where the invalid read occurs, indicating an off-by-one or [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marray boundary miscalculation.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Precise Location**: The overflow occurs exactly at the boundary of the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Curl_seconds` global variable [0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m from the end[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, suggesting the code is [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempting to access an element beyond the array bounds.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Memory Layout**: The shadow bytes show that the address `[0m[1;36m0x564a3c294240[0m[39m` is [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmarked as `f9` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mGlobal redzone[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, confirming that this is protected memory [0m          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m653[0m[39m:  [0m[35m/[0m[39m* thread-safe version *[0m[35m/[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m654[0m[39m:  tm = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstruct tm *[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35mgmtime_r[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&intime, store[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m655[0m[39m:#else[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m656[0m[39m:  [0m[35m/[0m[39m* !checksrc! disable BANNEDFUNC [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m657[0m[39m:  tm = [0m[1;35mgmtime[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&intime[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m658[0m[39m:  [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtm[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m659[0m[39m:    *store = *tm; [0m[35m/[0m[39m* copy the pointed struct to the local copy *[0m[35m/[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m660[0m[39m:#endif[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m661[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m662[0m[39m:  [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39m!tm[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m663[0m[39m:    return CURLE_BAD_FUNCTION_ARGUMENT;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m664[0m[39m:  return CURLE_OK;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m665[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlib/ftp.[0m[1;92mc:2092[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2092[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2092[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mputenv[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"[0m[32mTZ[0m[32m=[0m[32mright[0m[32m/UTC"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter reviewing the evaluation report and code snippets, I can identify the root [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause and develop a comprehensive fix strategy:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Direct Cause**: At `lib/ftp.[0m[1;92mc:2107[0m[39m`, the code accesses [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Curl_seconds[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtm->tm_sec[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` without bounds checking. The `Curl_seconds` array has [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexactly [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m elements [0m[1;39m([0m[39mindices [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but `tm->tm_sec` can legally be [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m when [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrepresenting a leap second.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Enabling Condition**: At `lib/ftp.[0m[1;92mc:2092[0m[39m`, the code explicitly sets [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mputenv[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"[0m[32mTZ[0m[32m=[0m[32mright[0m[32m/UTC"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which enables leap second support. This causes [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Curl_gmtime` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwrapping `gmtime_r`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to potentially return `[0m[33mtm_sec[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m60[0m[39m`.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Validation Gap**: The `ftp_213_date` function at line [0m[1;36m2021[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2023[0m[39m correctly [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidates that seconds can be <= [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m, acknowledging leap seconds. However, this [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation is not enforced before array indexing.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Codebase Patterns**: Other array accesses in the same code use defensive [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatterns:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `Curl_wkday[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtm->tm_wday ? tm->tm_wday-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m6[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m2101[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - adjusts index [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmapping[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `Curl_month[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtm->tm_mon[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m2103[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - direct access but tm_mon range [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m11[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmatches array size [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m12[0m[39m elements[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Context**: This code is part of `CURL_FTP_HTTPSTYLE_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39m` feature [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdefined at [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m310[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which the maintainers have already marked as [0m[32m"not elegant"[0m[39m, [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"error-prone"[0m[39m, and [0m[32m"subject for removal"[0m[39m. The vulnerable code tries to spell out [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mseconds as words [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[32m"twenty-six"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for aesthetic HTTP-style headers in FTP [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresponses.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Fix Strategy[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Primary Fix Location**: `lib/ftp.[0m[1;92mc:2107[0m[39m`[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix must clamp `tm->tm_sec` to the valid array index range [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before using [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit to access the `Curl_seconds` array. When `tm_sec` is [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mleap second[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, it should[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe clamped to [0m[1;36m59[0m[39m to prevent buffer overflow.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Implementation Steps**:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Modify line [0m[1;36m2107[0m[39m in `lib/ftp.c` to add bounds checking using a ternary operator [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mconsistent with the codebase pattern for `Curl_wkday`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Curl_seconds[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtm->tm_sec > [0m[1;36m59[0m[39m ? [0m[1;36m59[0m[39m : tm->tm_sec[0m[1;39m][0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This approach:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Clamps leap seconds [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m60[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to [0m[1;36m59[0m[39m, using [0m[32m"fifty-nine"[0m[39m as the textual [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrepresentation[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Maintains backward compatibility for normal seconds [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Uses a pattern already established in the same function for `Curl_wkday`[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Adds minimal performance overhead [0m[1;39m([0m[39msingle comparison[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Alternative approach** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif more explicit handling is preferred[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Add a local variable before the msnprintf call:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   int safe_sec = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtm->tm_sec > [0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;36m59[0m[39m : tm->tm_sec;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Then use `Curl_seconds[0m[1;39m[[0m[39msafe_sec[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` in the format string.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why This Is Optimal**:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal Impact**: The fix is localized to a single line in a single function, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mminimizing risk to the broader codebase.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Preserves Functionality**: [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The MDTM response processing continues to work correctly[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Time comparisons and conditional transfers remain unaffected[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Only the textual representation of leap seconds changes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfrom potential crash [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto showing [0m[32m"fifty-nine"[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Consistent with Codebase Patterns**: Uses the ternary operator pattern already[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39memployed for `Curl_wkday` array access in the same function.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No Harness Modifications**: The fix is entirely in the source code, not in [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzing infrastructure or test harnesses.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Handles Edge Case Gracefully**: When a leap second occurs [0m[1;39m([0m[33mtm_sec[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m60[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformatted header will show [0m[32m"fifty-nine seconds"[0m[39m instead of [0m[32m"sixty seconds"[0m[39m. This is[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39macceptable because:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Leap seconds are extremely rare[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This is cosmetic output in a deprecated feature[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The numeric timestamp [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`data->info.filetime`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains accurate[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other protocols [0m[1;39m([0m[39mHTTP, FILE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m use numeric formatting [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`%02d`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which would [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly show [0m[32m"60"[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **No External Dependencies**: The fix doesn't require changes to external [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibraries, timezone handling, or the `Curl_gmtime` wrapper.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. **Preserves Leap Second Awareness**: The `[0m[33mTZ[0m[39m=[0m[35mright[0m[39m/UTC` setting remains, so leap[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mseconds are still handled correctly in time calculations. Only the textual spelling[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis affected.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effects and Mitigation**:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Side Effect**: During an actual leap second, the formatted header will show [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"fifty-nine"[0m[39m instead of [0m[32m"sixty"[0m[39m.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: This is acceptable as the feature is deprecated and the impact[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis purely cosmetic. The underlying timestamp remains accurate.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Side Effect**: No impact on other time formatting code paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39mHTTP, FILE, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mGnuTLS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m since they use numeric formatting.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Verification**: Confirmed by examining `lib/http.[0m[1;92mc:1454[0m[39m`, `lib/file.[0m[1;92mc:498[0m[39m`, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`lib/vtls/gtls.[0m[1;92mc:203[0m[39m` which all use `%02d` for `tm->tm_sec`.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Side Effect**: No impact on time-based conditional transfers since those use [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe numeric `data->info.filetime` value.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Verification**: Confirmed by examining lines [0m[1;36m2126[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2150[0m[39m which perform time [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomparisons using the timestamp, not the formatted string.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative Solutions Considered and Rejected**:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Extend `Curl_seconds` array to [0m[1;36m61[0m[39m elements**: Would require adding a 61st [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39melement [0m[32m"sixty"[0m[39m to the array in `lib/parsedate.c`. Rejected because:[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Adds permanent overhead for an extremely rare case[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The feature is deprecated and may be removed[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Inconsistent with the maintainers' stated desire to remove this feature[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Remove leap second support**: Change timezone from [0m[32m"right/UTC"[0m[39m to [0m[32m"GMT"[0m[39m. [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRejected because:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Would affect time accuracy in other parts of the code[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Tests explicitly warn about [0m[32m"right"[0m[39m timezones affecting other features[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The intent is clearly to support accurate time representation[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Add array size check with fallback**: Use a conditional to check if [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tm->tm_sec >= [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m` and use a static string. Rejected because:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - More complex than needed[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ternary operator is simpler and sufficient[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Test Compatibility**:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix will not break existing tests because:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
